The details of this locking are:\n256:       //  - Hosts are not thread local, they are global.\n257:       //  - We take a read lock when reading the address and a write lock when changing it.\n258:       //  - Address updates are very rare.\n259:       //  - Address reads are only done when a connection is being made and a \"real\" host\n260:       //    description is created or the host is queried via the admin endpoint. Both of\n261:       //    these operations are relatively rare and the read lock is held for a short period\n262:       //    of time.\n263:       //\n264:       // TODO(mattklein123): Right now the dynamic forward proxy / DNS cache works similar to how\n265:       //                     logical DNS works, meaning that we only store a single address per\n266:       //                     resolution. Now I understand the issue. In `updateCrossPriorityHostMap`:\n1. When hosts are removed, they are erased from the map using `addressToString(host->address())`\n2. When hosts are added, they are inserted using `addressToString(host->address())`\n\nThe current code in cluster.cc (line 273-276) calls `setNewAddresses()` on the existing LogicalHost, which updates the address in-place. This means:\n1. When a host resolves to IP A first, it gets added to the cross-priority host map with key \"A\"\n2. When it resolves to IP B later, `setNewAddresses()` is called (no callbacks)\n3. But the old entry in the cross-priority host map with key \"A\" is never removed\n4. The new address B is also never added to the map because there's no callback event\n\nThe fix needs to:\n1. Remove the old host and create a new one instead of in-place update\n2. This will trigger both hosts_removed and hosts_added events\n3. These events will properly update the cross-priority host map\n\nNow let me understand what changes need to be made. Based on the description:1. Simplify `addOrUpdateHost()` signature to remove the `hosts_added` out-parameter\n2. Make `addOrUpdateHost()` call `updatePriorityState()` directly\n3. {\n244:     absl::WriterMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};\n245: \n246:     // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have\n247:     // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n248:     // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is\n249:     // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on\n250:     // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. We may have to revisit this in the\n251:     // future.\n252:     const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);\n253:     if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {\n254:       // If we only have an address change, we can do that swap inline without any other updates.\n255:       // The appropriate R/W locking is in place to allow this. The details of this locking are:\n256:       //  - Hosts are not thread local, they are global.\n257:       //  - We take a read lock when reading the address and a write lock when changing it.\n258:       //  - Address updates are very rare.\n259:       //  - Address reads are only done when a connection is being made and a \"real\" host\n260:       //    description is created or the host is queried via the admin endpoint. Both of\n261:       //    these operations are relatively rare and the read lock is held for a short period\n262:       //    of time.\n263:       //\n264:       // TODO(mattklein123): Right now the dynamic forward proxy / DNS cache works similar to how\n265:       //                     logical DNS works, meaning that we only store a single address per\n266:       //                     resolution. It would not be difficult to also expose strict DNS\n267:       //                     semantics, meaning the cache would expose multiple addresses and the\n268:       //                     cluster would create multiple logical hosts based on those addresses.\n269:       //                     We will leave this is a follow up depending on need.\n270:       ASSERT(host_info == ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cluster='{}' TTL expired\", cluster_name_);\n    return true;\n  }\n  return false;\n}\n\nvoid Cluster::addOrUpdateHost(\n    absl::string_view host,\n    const Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& host_info) {\n  Upstream::HostVector hosts_added;\n  Upstream::HostVector hosts_removed;\n  {\n    absl::WriterMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};\n\n    // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have\n    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is\n    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on\n    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. We may have to revisit this in the\n    // future.\n    const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);\n    if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {\n      // If we have an address change, remove the old host and create a new one.\n      // This ensures proper updates to the cross-priority host map.\n      ASSERT(host_info == host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_);\n      if (host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_->address() !=\n          host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address()) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"updating dfproxy cluster host address '{}'\", host);\n        // Collect the old host for removal\n        hosts_removed.emplace_back(host_map_it->second.logical_host_);\n        host_map_.erase(host_map_it);\n\n        // Create a new host with the updated address\n        auto emplaced_host =\n            host_map_\n                .try_emplace(host, host_info,\n                             std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(\n                                 info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                 host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n                                 dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                .first->second.logical_host_;\n        hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n      }\n      // If address didn't change, do nothing\n      return;\n    }\n\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"adding new dfproxy cluster host '{}'\", host);\n\n    auto emplaced_host = host_map_\n                             .try_emplace(host, host_info,\n                                          std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(\n                                              info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                              host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n                                              dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                             .first->second.logical_host_;\n    hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n  }\n\n  if (!hosts_added.empty() || !hosts_removed.empty()) {\n    updatePriorityState(hosts_added, hosts_removed);\n  }\n}\n\nvoid Cluster::onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\n    const std::string& host,\n    const Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& host_info) {\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Adding host info for {}\", host);\n  addOrUpdateHost(host, host_info);\n}\n\nvoid Cluster::updatePriorityState(const Upstream::HostVector& hosts_added,\n                                  const Upstream::HostVector& hosts_removed) {\n  Upstream::PriorityStateManager priority_state_manager(*this, local_info_, nullptr);\n  priority_state_manager.initializePriorityFor(dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_);\n  {\n    absl::ReaderMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};\n    for (const auto& host : host_map_) {\n      priority_state_manager.registerHostForPriority(host.second.logical_host_,\n                                                     dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_);\n    }\n  }\n  priority_state_manager.updateClusterPrioritySet(\n      0, std::move(priority_state_manager.priorityState()[0].first), hosts_added, hosts_removed);\n}\n\nUpstream::HostConstSharedPtr\nCluster::LoadBalancer::chooseHost(Upstream::LoadBalancerContext* context) {\n  if (!context) {\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n\n  const context->requestStreamInfo()->filterState().getDataReadOnly<Router::StringAccessor>(\n            DynamicHostFilterStateKey);\n  }\n\n  absl::string_view raw_host;\n  if (dynamic_host_filter_state) (context->downstreamConnection()) {\n    raw_host = context->downstreamConnection()->requestedServerName();\n  }\n\n  // For host lookup, we need to make sure to match the host of any DNS cache\n  // insert. Two code points currently do DNS cache insert: the http DFP filter,\n  // which inserts for HTTP traffic, and sets port based on the cluster's\n  // security level, and the SNI DFP network filter which sets port based on\n  // stream metadata, or configuration (which is then added as stream metadata).\n  const bool is_secure = cluster_.info()\n                             ->transportSocketMatcher()\n                             .resolve(nullptr)\n                             .factory_.implementsSecureTransport();\n  uint32_t port = is_secure ? 443 : 80;\n  if }\n}\n\nabsl::optional<Upstream::SelectedPoolAndConnection>\nCluster::LoadBalancer::selectExistingConnection(Upstream::LoadBalancerContext* /*context*/,\n lock{&host_map_lock_};\n\n    // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have\n    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is\n    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on\n    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. We may have to revisit this in the\n    // future.\n    const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);\n    if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {\n      // If we have an address change, remove the old host and create a new one.\n      // This ensures proper updates to the cross-priority host map.\n      ASSERT(host_info == host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_);\n      if (host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_->address() !=\n          host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address()) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"updating dfproxy cluster host address '{}'\", host);\n             info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                 host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n .first->second.logical_host_;\n    hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n  }\n\n  if (!hosts_added.empty() || !hosts_removed.empty()) {\n    updatePriorityState(hosts_added, hosts_removed);\n \"fake_cluster_name\";\n  const std::string host = \"localhost\";\n  const int port = 80;\n  std::pair<bool, absl::optional<envoy::config::cluster::v3::Cluster>> sub_cluster_pair =\n      cluster_->createSubClusterConfig(cluster_name, host, port);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.first);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.second.has_value());\n\n  // create again, already exists\n of the cluster including adding hosts and removing them.\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, BasicFlow) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"\")));\n\n  // Verify no host LB cases.\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->peekAnotherHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n\n  // LB will immediately resolve host1.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // After changing the address, LB will immediately resolve the new address with a refresh.\n  updateTestHostAddress(\"host1:0\", \"2.3.4.5\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Remove the host, LB will immediately fail to find the host in the map.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(0), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostRemove(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(0UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n}\n\n// Outlier detection\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, OutlierDetection) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  makeTestHost(\"host2:0\", \"5.6.7.8\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host2:0\", host_map_[\"host2:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Fail outlier check for host1\n  setOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n  // \"host2:0\" should not be affected\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Clear outlier check failure for host1, it should be available again\n  clearOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n}\n\n// Various invalid LB orig_cluster_config_;\n\n  // Overwrite the type.\n  config.set_name(cluster_name);\n  config.clear_cluster_type();\n  config.set_lb_policy(sub_cluster_lb_policy_);\n  config.set_type(\n      envoy::config::cluster::v3::Cluster_DiscoveryType::Cluster_DiscoveryType_STRICT_DNS);\n\n  // Set endpoint.\n  auto load_assignments = config.mutable_load_assignment();\n  load_assignments->set_cluster_name(cluster_name);\n  load_assignments->clear_endpoints();\n\n  auto socket_address = load_assignments->add_endpoints()\n                            ->add_lb_endpoints()\n                            ->mutable_endpoint()\n                            ->mutable_address()\n                            ->mutable_socket_address();\n  socket_address->set_address(host);\n  socket_address->set_port_value(port);\n\n  return std::make_pair(true, absl::make_optional(config));\n}\n\nUpstream::HostConstSharedPtr Cluster::chooseHost(absl::string_view host,\n                                                 Upstream::LoadBalancerContext* context) const {\n  uint16_t default_port = 80;\n  if cluster_name_);\n  last_used_time_ = parent_.time_source_.monotonicTime().time_since_epoch();\n}\n\n// checkIdle run in the main thread.\nbool Cluster::ClusterInfo::checkIdle() {\n  ASSERT(parent_.main_thread_dispatcher_.isThreadSafe());\n\n  const std::chrono::steady_clock::duration now_duration =\n      parent_.main_thread_dispatcher_.timeSource().monotonicTime().time_since_epoch();\n  auto last_used_time = last_used_time_.load();\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cluster='{}' TTL check: now={} last_used={} TTL lock{&host_map_lock_};\n\n    // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have\n    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is\n    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on\n    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. We may have to revisit this in the\n    // future.\n    const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);\n    if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {\n      // If we have an address change, remove the old host and create a new one.\n      // This ensures proper updates to the cross-priority host map.\n      ASSERT(host_info == host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_);\n      if (host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_->address() !=\n          host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address()) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"updating dfproxy cluster host address '{}'\", host);\n        // Collect the old host for removal\n        hosts_removed.emplace_back(host_map_it->second.logical_host_);\n        host_map_.erase(host_map_it);\n\n        // Create a new host with the updated address\n        auto emplaced_host =\n            host_map_\n                .try_emplace(host, host_info,\n                             std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(\n                                 info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                 host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n                                 dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                .first->second.logical_host_;\n        hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n      }\n      // If address didn't change, do nothing\n      return;\n    }\n\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"adding new dfproxy cluster host '{}'\", host);\n\n    auto emplaced_host = host_map_\n                             .try_emplace(host, host_info,\n                                          std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(\n                                              info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                              host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n                                              dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                             .first->second.logical_host_;\n    hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n  }\n\n  if (!hosts_added.empty() || !hosts_removed.empty()) {\n    updatePriorityState(hosts_added, hosts_removed);\n  }\n}\n\nvoid Cluster::onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\n    const std::string& host,\n    const Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& host_info) {\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Adding host info ASSERT(parent_.main_thread_dispatcher_.isThreadSafe());\n\n  const std::chrono::steady_clock::duration now_duration =\n      parent_.main_thread_dispatcher_.timeSource().monotonicTime().time_since_epoch();\n  auto last_used_time = last_used_time_.load();\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cluster='{}' TTL check: now={} last_used={} TTL Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& host_info) {\n  Upstream::HostVector hosts_added;\n  Upstream::HostVector hosts_removed;\n  {\n    absl::WriterMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};\n\n    // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have\n    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is\n    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on\n    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. We may have to revisit this in the\n    // future.\n    const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);\n    if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {\n      // If we have an address change, remove the old host and create a new one.\n      // This ensures proper updates to the cross-priority host map.\n      ASSERT(host_info == host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_);\n      if (host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_->address() !=\n          host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address()) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"updating dfproxy cluster host address '{}'\", host);\n        // Collect the old host for removal\n        hosts_removed.emplace_back(host_map_it->second.logical_host_);\n        host_map_.erase(host_map_it);\n\n        // Create a new host with the updated address\n        auto emplaced_host =\n            host_map_\n                .try_emplace(host, host_info,\n                             std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(\n                                 info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                 host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n                                 dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                .first->second.logical_host_;\n        hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n        // Unlock before calling updatePriorityState to avoid deadlock\n      }\n      // If address didn't change, do nothing\n      if (hosts_added.empty() && hosts_removed.empty()) {\n        return;\n      }\n    } else {\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"adding new dfproxy cluster host '{}'\", host);\n\n      auto emplaced_host = host_map_\n                               .try_emplace(host, host_info,\n                                            std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(\n                                                info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                                host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n                                                dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                               .first->second.logical_host_;\n      hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (!hosts_added.empty() || !hosts_removed.empty()) {\n    updatePriorityState(hosts_added, hosts_removed);\n  }\n}\n\nvoid Cluster::onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\n    const std::string& host,\n    const Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& host_info) {\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, lock{&host_map_lock_};\n\n    // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have\n    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is\n    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on\n    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. We may have to revisit this in the\n    // future.\n    const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);\n    if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {\n      // If we have an address change, remove the old host and create a new one.\n      // This ensures proper updates to the cross-priority host map.\n      ASSERT(host_info == host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_);\n      if (host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_->address() !=\n          host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address()) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"updating dfproxy cluster host address '{}'\", host);\n             info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                 host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n                                 dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                .first->second.logical_host_;\n        hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n        // Unlock before calling updatePriorityState to avoid deadlock\n      }\n      // If address didn't change, do nothing\n      if (hosts_added.empty() && hosts_removed.empty()) {\n        return;\n      }\n    } else {\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, .first->second.logical_host_;\n      hosts_added.emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (!hosts_added.empty() || !hosts_removed.empty()) {\n    updatePriorityState(hosts_added,
